## What I would do next (process)
- Treat this as a **“breakout readiness” list**, not a buy list.  
- Require **SEPA breakout confirmation**: **close ≥ pivot + 2%** *and* **volume ≥ 1.2x–1.5x** (ideally more for the weaker RS names).  
- **Prioritize RS leaders** (GLE.PA, SAN.MC, BBVA.MC, INGA.AS, UCG.MI) because SEPA winners usually come from leadership.

If you want, I can also:
1) Flag which of these are **too extended/late-stage** vs “first/second stage base” (needs longer-term chart context), and  
2) Build a **single unified watchlist** combining A-list + pre-breakout list, sorted by “distance to pivot” and “RS quality.”
